 Two things are most important in the budget, one is transparency and second is public participation

 Transparency India International has said in its report that there is a system of estimating the budget of countries around the world in the Open Budget Survey on the scale of transparency
 2017 ke survey main bharat kaa 115 deshon main 53 waan sthaan rahaa
 This institution ranked India 48 out of 100 in budget transparency and 15 out of 100 on public participation in the budget, and 48 in budget oversight
 isi sanstha ne yah suzav bhi diya gaya tha, ki paardarshita ke liye bajet se pehlevivernon ko saarvajanik kiya jaae, isaki chamahi samiksha bhi ho

 The organization has said that it is unfortunate for the country that apart from the Union Budget, the state budget has never been given priority, only the Union Budget has been given priority and every year it has been the subject of strong discussion and observation in the Parliament
 vahi duusari taraf bagaiyr kisi saamaajik charchaa ke rajya sarkaron dwaara bhartiya rajyon main bajet prastut hote rahe he
 As a result, state governments continued to prepare less transparent budgets

 ‚Äúin the context of budget and treasury, decisions taken by the state governments have more power to influence the citizens than the center

 On the occasion of the 145th birth anniversary of Mahatma Gandhi, a question flashes again - is Gandhi relevant even in the 21st century? Niranjan Ramakrishnan, of Tamil origin, based in Portland, Oregon, an American 'sanctuary' of 21st century technology - published by Palgrave Macmillan, New York, 2013 - in his new book 'reading Gandhi in the Twenty First Century' (reading Gandhi in the 21st Century; This book is going to be launched in India soon)
 unka kahana he, mere vichaar main gandhi jayanti manaane kaa sabase upyukt tarika he, yah pustak 12veen kaksha tathaa snaatak kar rahe sabhi vidhyaarthiyon ko muft vitarit kii jaae (jahaan in 138 prishthon ke anuwaad kii zarurat ho, kiya jaae), taaki agali peedi kaa prayek vyakti apane-aap is sawaal kaa jawaab talash karne kii koshish kar sake

 ponting ne us samay kaha tha, meri hameshaa se yah raay rahi he ki main jin ballebaajon ke saath yaa khilaaf khelaa, unamem vah (tendulkar) sarvshereshth he
 If we look at the old matches, in fact they won matches against us on several occasions on their own
 tendulkar or lara donon ne australia ke khilaaf acha pradarshan kiya he, lekin is desh ke adhiktar cricketron kii najar main bhartiya ballebaaj behatar he

 vahiin duusari taraf kabhi vidhaan parishad main bahumat rakhane vaali bispi is chunaav main do siten hasil kar saki
 Now only 16 members are left in the Upper House
 iske alaava bijepi kaa ek bhi pratyaashee vidhaan parishad chunaav main kaamyaab nahin ho sakaa
 It now has seven members in the Upper House
 tippaniyan After Dinesh Singh won re-election in Rae Bareli, the number of Congress members has again increased to two
 iske alaava sadan main shikshak dal ke paanch, nirdaleey samooh ke chah tathaa rashtriya lokdal kaa ek sadsy he, jabaki paanch siten rikt hai
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Of the 36 seats in the local authority area, eight candidates of the SP were declared unopposed on 18 February itself
 baaki bachi 28 siton ke liye teen march ko hue chunaav ke ghoshit parinaamon ke anusaar espi pramukh mulaayam singh yadav ke sansadeey nirvachan kshetra azamgarh main party pratyaashee rakesh yadav ne apane nikatatam pratidwandvi bijepi ke rajesh singh ko parajeet kiya
 At the same time, in Badaun, SP candidate Banwari Singh Yadav defeated Jitendra Yadav of BJP
 pradhanmantri narendra modi ke sansadeey nirvachan kshetra varanasi main nirdaleey pratyaashee mafia don brijesh singh ne espi pratyaashee minaa singh ko parajeet kiya
 In the Rae Bareli constituency of Congress President Sonia Gandhi, party candidate Dinesh Pratap Singh won
 bispi ko jonpur or saharanpur siton par kamyaabi hasil hui
 In Jaunpur, his candidates Brijesh Singh alias Prince and Mahmood Ali won the muzaffarnagar-saharanpur seat
 iske saath hi sattarudh sapa ko 100 sadasyeey vidhaan parishad main bhi bahumat hasil ho gaya he
 The SP had 27 members in the House before this election
 espi ke aath pratyaashee pehle hi nirvirodh ghoshit hue the
 Now SP has won 23 more seats in the election
 is tarah ucch sadan main uske sadasyon kii sankhya 58 ho gai he
 On the other hand, the BSP, which once held a majority in the Legislative Council, could win two seats in this election
 ab ucch sadan main uske sirf 16 sadsy hi rah gayi hai
 Apart from this, not a single BJP candidate could succeed in the Legislative Council elections
 ucch sadan main ab uske paas saat sadsy hai
 The comments raibareli main dinesh singh ke dobaaraa chunaav jeetne ke baad congress ke sadasyon kii sankhya phir do ho gayi he
 Apart from this, there are five teachers in the house, six members of the independent group and one member of the National Lok Dal, while five seats are vacant

 Let's know some special things about Salim Khan of salim-javed, the famous couple of 70s and 80s
 1
 Salim Khan was born on 24 November 1935 in Indore
 2
 Salim Khan's father used to be a police officer and his mother died in childhood
 3
 Salim Khan married a Marathi girl Sushila Charak in 1964 who was later named Salma Khan
